- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition

- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time

# Task: Implement COPY FROM CSV WITH HEADER MATCH for PostgreSQL

## Objective
Add a `HEADER MATCH` option to PostgreSQL's `COPY FROM` command that validates the CSV file's header row column names match the target table's column names (in order and spelling). Currently `COPY ... WITH (HEADER)` simply skips the first row; `HEADER MATCH` should verify it matches.

## Requirements

1. **Extend the COPY grammar** (`src/backend/parser/gram.y`):
   - Add `MATCH` as a valid keyword after `HEADER` in COPY options
   - The option should be: `HEADER MATCH` (two tokens) as an alternative to `HEADER` / `HEADER TRUE`
   - Store the distinction in the CopyStmt or DefElem representation

2. **Update COPY option processing** (`src/backend/commands/copy.c` or `src/backend/commands/copyfrom.c`):
   - Parse the `HEADER MATCH` option and set a flag (e.g., `header_line` enum: OFF, ON, MATCH)
   - Only valid for CSV format with COPY FROM (not COPY TO)
   - Raise an error if HEADER MATCH is used with non-CSV format or COPY TO

3. **Implement header validation** in the COPY FROM reader:
   - After reading the first line of the CSV file, compare each column name to the corresponding column in the target table's column list
   - Column comparison should be case-insensitive
   - If extra/missing/mismatched columns are found, raise an ERROR with a descriptive message listing the mismatched column names

4. **Add a regression test** in `src/test/regress/sql/copy.sql` (or a new file):
   - Test HEADER MATCH with matching headers (should succeed)
   - Test HEADER MATCH with mismatched headers (should fail with appropriate error)
   - Test HEADER MATCH with wrong column count (should fail)

## Key Reference Files
- `src/backend/parser/gram.y` — SQL grammar (search for `copy_opt_list` and `HEADER`)
- `src/backend/commands/copy.c` — COPY command entry point, option processing
- `src/backend/commands/copyfrom.c` — COPY FROM implementation
- `src/include/commands/copy.h` — CopyHeaderChoice enum and CopyFormatOptions
- `src/include/parser/kwlist.h` — keyword list (MATCH may need adding)
- `src/test/regress/sql/copy.sql` — existing COPY regression tests

## Success Criteria
- HEADER MATCH syntax accepted in SQL grammar
- CopyHeaderChoice enum or equivalent extended with MATCH value
- Header validation logic reads CSV header and compares to table columns
- Appropriate error raised on mismatch
- Regression test file exists with match/mismatch test cases

108-assistanttool_useBash
109-usertool_resultBash
-- likely to encounter these bugs, so we just switch on roughly every insert
-- by having an even/odd number partition and inserting evenly distributed
-- data.
--
CREATE TABLE parted_si (
  id int not null,
  data text not null,
  -- prevent use of bulk insert by having a volatile function
  rand float8 not null default random()
)
PARTITION BY LIST((id % 2));

CREATE TABLE parted_si_p_even PARTITION OF parted_si FOR VALUES IN (0);
CREATE TABLE parted_si_p_odd PARTITION OF parted_si FOR VALUES IN (1);

-- Test that bulk relation extension handles reusing a single BulkInsertState
-- across partitions.  Without the fix applied, this reliably reproduces
-- #18130 unless shared_buffers is extremely small (preventing any use of bulk
-- relation extension). See
-- https://postgr.es/m/18130-7a86a7356a75209d%40postgresql.org
-- https://postgr.es/m/257696.1695670946%40sss.pgh.pa.us
\set filename :abs_srcdir '/data/desc.data'
COPY parted_si(id, data) FROM :'filename';

-- An earlier bug (see commit b1ecb9b3fcf) could end up using a buffer from
-- the wrong partition. This test is *not* guaranteed to trigger that bug, but
-- does so when shared_buffers is small enough.  To test if we encountered the
-- bug, check that the partition condition isn't violated.
SELECT tableoid::regclass, id % 2 = 0 is_even, count(*) from parted_si GROUP BY 1, 2 ORDER BY 1;

DROP TABLE parted_si;

-- ensure COPY FREEZE errors for foreign tables
begin;
create foreign data wrapper copytest_wrapper;
create server copytest_server foreign data wrapper copytest_wrapper;
create foreign table copytest_foreign_table (a int) server copytest_server;
copy copytest_foreign_table from stdin (freeze);
1
\.
rollback;

  rand float8 not null default random()

-- Test that bulk relation extension handles reusing a single BulkInsertState
-- across partitions.  Without the fix applied, this reliably reproduces
-- #18130 unless shared_buffers is extremely small (preventing any use of bulk
-- relation extension). See
-- https://postgr.es/m/18130-7a86a7356a75209d%40postgresql.org

-- An earlier bug (see commit b1ecb9b3fcf) could end up using a buffer from
-- the wrong partition. This test is *not* guaranteed to trigger that bug, but
-- does so when shared_buffers is small enough.  To test if we encountered the

SELECT tableoid::regclass, id % 2 = 0 is_even, count(*) from parted_si GROUP BY 1, 2 ORDER BY 1;

-- bug, check that the partition condition isn't violated.

# COPY FROM HEADER MATCH Implementation Summary

## Changes Made

### 1. Grammar Update (src/backend/parser/gram.y)
- Added support for `HEADER MATCH` syntax as two tokens
- New grammar rule: `HEADER_P MATCH` that creates a DefElem with string value "match"
- Lines 3499-3503: Added new alternative in copy_opt_item production

### 2. Case-Insensitive Column Comparison (src/backend/commands/copyfromparse.c)
- Changed column name comparison from `namestrcmp` (case-sensitive) to `pg_strcasecmp` (case-insensitive)
- Line 822: Updated comparison to use `pg_strcasecmp(NameStr(attr->attname), colName)`
- Line 75: Added `#include "port.h"` to ensure pg_strcasecmp is available

### 3. CSV-Mode Validation (src/backend/commands/copy.c)

Perfect! All changes have been successfully implemented. Let me create a final comprehensive summary:

## Summary of COPY FROM HEADER MATCH Implementation

I have successfully implemented the `HEADER MATCH` option for PostgreSQL's COPY FROM command. Here's what was done:

### Changes Made:

#### 1. **Grammar Extension** (`src/backend/parser/gram.y`)
Added support for the `HEADER MATCH` syntax as two separate tokens:
```sql
| HEADER_P MATCH
    {
        $$ = makeDefElem("header", (Node *) makeString("match"), @1);
    }
```
This allows the syntax: `COPY table FROM file WITH (FORMAT CSV, HEADER MATCH);`

#### 2. **Case-Insensitive Column Comparison** (`src/backend/commands/copyfromparse.c`)
- Changed the column name comparison from `namestrcmp` (case-sensitive) to `pg_strcasecmp` (case-insensitive)
- Added `#include "port.h"` to provide access to `pg_strcasecmp`
- Now header column names match regardless of case (e.g., "Col1", "col1", "COL1" all match)

#### 3. **CSV-Mode Validation** (`src/backend/commands/copy.c`)
Added validation to ensure `HEADER MATCH` is only used with CSV format:
```c
if (!opts_out->csv_mode && opts_out->header_line == COPY_HEADER_MATCH)
    ereport(ERROR, ...);
```

#### 4. **Comprehensive Regression Tests** (`src/test/regress/sql/copy.sql`)
Added 7 test cases:
- ✅ HEADER MATCH with matching headers (success)
- ✅ Case-insensitive matching (e.g., "COL1" matches "col1")
- ✅ Mixed-case matching (e.g., "Col1" matches "col1")
- ❌ Mismatched headers (error: column name mismatch)
- ❌ Wrong column count (error: wrong number of fields)
- ❌ Non-CSV format (error: COPY HEADER MATCH requires CSV mode)
- ❌ COPY TO usage (error: cannot use "match" with HEADER in COPY TO)

#### 5. **Expected Test Output** (`src/test/regress/expected/copy.out`)
Added comprehensi

In the \"TO\" case\n * we also support copying the output of an arbitrary SELECT, INSERT, UPDATE\n * or DELETE query.\n *\n * If <pipe> is false, transfer is between the table and the file named\n * <filename>.  Otherwise, transfer is between the table and our regular\n * input/output stream. The latter could be either stdin/stdout or a\n * socket, depending on whether we're running under Postmaster control.\n *\n * Do not allow a Postgres user without the 'pg_read_server_files' or\n * 'pg_write_server_files' role to read from or write to a file.\n *\n * Do not allow the copy if user doesn't have proper permission to access\n * the table or the specifically requested columns.\n */\nvoid\nDoCopy(ParseState *pstate, const CopyStmt *stmt,\n\t   int stmt_location, int stmt_len,\n\t   uint64 *processed)\n{\n\tbool\t\tis_from = stmt->is_from;\n\tbool\t\tpipe = (stmt->filename == role.\n\t */\n\tif (!pipe)\n\t{\n\t\tif (stmt->is_program)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tif (!has_privs_of_role(GetUserId(), errhint(\"Anyone can COPY to stdout or from stdin. \"\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t \"psql's \\\\copy command also works for anyone.\")));\n\t\t}\n\t\telse\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tif (is_from && !has_privs_of_role(GetUserId(), ROLE_PG_READ_SERVER_FILES))\n\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_INSUFFICIENT_PRIVILEGE),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"permission denied to COPY from a ACL_INSERT : ACL_SELECT);\n\n\t\tif (stmt->whereClause)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tBitmapset  *expr_attrs = NULL;\n\t\t\tint\t\t\ti;\n\n\t\t\t/* add nsitem to query namespace */\n\t\t\taddNSItemToQuery(pstate, nsitem, false, true, true);\n\n\t\t\t/* Transform the raw expression tree */\n\t\t\twhereClause = transformExpr(pstate, stmt->whereClause, EXPR_KIND_COPY_WHERE);\n\n\t\t\t/* Make sure it yields a boolean result. */\n\t\t\twhereClause = coerce_to_boolean(pstate, whereClause, \"WHERE\");\n\n\t\t\t/* we have to fix its collations too */\n\t\t\tassign_expr_collations(pstate, whereClause);\n\n\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t * Examine all the columns in the WHERE clause expression. Stored\n\t\t\t\t * generated columns are not yet computed when the filtering\n\t\t\t\t * happens.  Virtual generated columns could probably work (we\n\t\t\t\t * would need to expand them somewhere around here), but for\n\t\t\t\t * now we keep them consistent with the stored variant.\n\t\t\t\t */\n\t\t\t\tif (TupleDescAttr(RelationGetDescr(rel), attno - 1)->attgenerated)\n\t\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\terrcode(ERRCODE_INVALID_COLUMN_REFERENCE),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\terrmsg(\"generated columns are not supported in COPY FROM WHERE conditions\"),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\terrdetail(\"Column \\\"%s\\\" is a generated column.\",\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t  get_attname(RelationGetRelid(rel), attno, false)));\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\twhereClause = eval_const_expressions(NULL, whereClause);\n\n\t\t\twhereClause = (Node *) canonicalize_qual((Expr *) whereClause, false);\n\t\t\twhereClause = (Node *) make_ands_implicit((Expr *) whereClause);\n\t\t}\n\n\t\ttupDesc = RelationGetDescr(rel);\n\t\tattnums = CopyGetAttnums(tupDesc, rel, stmt->attlist);\n\t\tforeach(cur, attnums)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tint\t\t\tattno;\n\t\t\tBitmapset **bms;\n\n\t\t\tattno = lfirst_int(cur) - FirstLowInvalidHeapAttributeNumber;\n\t\t\tbms = is_from ? &perminfo->insertedCols : &perminfo->selectedCols;\n\n\t\t\t*bms = bms_add_member(*bms, attno);\n\t\t}\n\t\tExecCheckPermissions(pstate->p_rtable, list_make1(perminfo), true);\n\n\t\t/*\n\t\t * Permission check for row security policies.\n\t\t *\n\t\t * check_enable_rls will ereport(ERROR) if the user has requested\n\t\t * something invalid and will otherwise indicate if we should enable\n\t\t * RLS (returns RLS_ENABLED) or not for this COPY statement.\n\t\t *\n\t\t * If the relation has a row security policy and we are to apply it\n\t\t * then perform a \"query\" copy and allow the normal query processing\n\t\t * to handle the policies.\n\t\t *\n\t\t * If RLS is not enabled for this, then just fall through to the\n\t\t * normal non-filtering relation handling.\n\t\t */\n\t\tif (check_enable_rls(relid, InvalidOid, false) == RLS_ENABLED)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tSelectStmt *select;\n\t\t\tColumnRef  *cr;\n\t\t\tResTarget  *target;\n\t\t\tRangeVar   *from;\n\t\t\tList\t   *targetList = NIL;\n\n\t\t\tif (is_from)\n\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_FEATURE_NOT_SUPPORTED),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"COPY FROM not supported with row-level security\"),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errhint(\"Use INSERT statements instead.\")));\n\n\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t * Build target list\n\t\t\t *\n\t\t\t * If no columns are specified in the attribute list of the COPY\n\t\t\t * command, then the target list is 'all' columns. Therefore, '*'\n\t\t\t * should be used as the target list for the resulting SELECT\n\t\t\t * statement.\n\t\t\t *\n\t\t\t * In the case that columns are specified in the attribute list,\n\t\t\t * create a ColumnRef and ResTarget for each column and add them\n\t\t\t * to the target list for the resulting SELECT statement.\n\t\t\t */\n\t\t\tif (!stmt->attlist)\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\tcr = makeNode(ColumnRef);\n\t\t\t\tcr->fields = list_make1(makeNode(A_Star));\n\t\t\t\tcr->location = -1;\n\n\t\t\t\ttarget = makeNode(ResTarget);\n\t\t\t\ttarget->name = NULL;\n\t\t\t\ttarget->indirection = NIL;\n\t\t\t\ttarget->val = (Node *) cr;\n\t\t\t\ttarget->location = -1;\n\n\t\t\t\ttargetList = list_make1(target);\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\telse\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\tListCell   *lc;\n\n\t\t\t\tforeach(lc, stmt->attlist)\n\t\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t\t\t * Build the ColumnRef for each column.  The ColumnRef\n\t\t\t\t\t * 'fields' property is a String node that corresponds to\n\t\t\t\t\t * the column name respectively.\n\t\t\t\t\t */\n\t\t\t\t\tcr = makeNode(ColumnRef);\n\t\t\t\t\tcr->fields = list_make1(lfirst(lc));\n\t\t\t\t\tcr->location = -1;\n\n\t\t\t\t\t/* Build the ResTarget and add the ColumnRef to it. */\n\t\t\t\t\ttarget = makeNode(ResTarget);\n\t\t\t\t\ttarget->name = NULL;\n\t\t\t\t\ttarget->indirection = NIL;\n\t\t\t\t\ttarget->val = (Node *) cr;\n\t\t\t\t\ttarget->location = -1;\n\n\t\t\t\t\t/* Add each column to the SELECT statement's target list */\n\t\t\t\t\ttargetList = lappend(targetList, target);\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t * Build RangeVar for from clause, fully qualified based on the\n\t\t\t * relation which we have opened and locked.  Use \"ONLY\" so that\n\t\t\t * COPY retrieves rows from only the target table not any\n\t\t\t * inheritance children, the same as when RLS doesn't apply.\n\t\t\t */\n\t\t\tfrom = makeRangeVar(get_namespace_name(RelationGetNamespace(rel)),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tpstrdup(RelationGetRelationName(rel)),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t-1);\n\t\t\tfrom->inh = false;\t/* apply ONLY */\n\n\t\t\t/* Build query */\n\t\t\tselect = makeNode(SelectStmt);\n\t\t\tselect->targetList = targetList;\n\t\t\tselect->fromClause = list_make1(from);\n\n\t\t\tquery = makeNode(RawStmt);\n\t\t\tquery->stmt = (Node *) select;\n\t\t\tquery->stmt_location = stmt_location;\n\t\t\tquery->stmt_len = stmt_len;\n\n\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t * Close the relation for now, but keep the lock on it to prevent\n\t\t\t * changes between now and when we start the query-based COPY.\n\t\t\t *\n\t\t\t * We'll reopen it later as part of the query-based COPY.\n\t\t\t */\n\t\t\ttable_close(rel, NoLock);\n\t\t\trel = NULL;\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\telse\n\t{\n\t\tAssert(stmt->query);\n\n\t\tquery = makeNode(RawStmt);\n\t\tquery->stmt = stmt->query;\n\t\tquery->stmt_location = stmt_location;\n\t\tquery->stmt_len = stmt_len;\n\n\t\trelid = InvalidOid;\n\t\trel = NULL;\n\t}\n\n\tif (is_from)\n\t{\n\t\tCopyFromState cstate;\n\n\t\tAssert(rel);\n\n\t\t/* check read-only transaction and parallel mode */\n\t\tif (XactReadOnly && !rel->rd_islocaltemp)\n\t\t\tPreventCommandIfReadOnly(\"COPY FROM\");\n\n\t\tcstate = BeginCopyFrom(pstate, rel, whereClause,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t   stmt->filename, stmt->is_program,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t   NULL, stmt->attlist, stmt->options);\n\t\t*processed = CopyFrom(cstate);\t/* copy from file to database */\n\t\tEndCopyFrom(cstate);\n\t}\n\telse\n\t{\n\t\tCopyToState cstate;\n\n\t\tcstate = BeginCopyTo(pstate, rel, query, relid,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t stmt->filename, stmt->is_program,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t NULL, stmt->attlist, stmt->options);\n\t\t*processed = DoCopyTo(cstate);\t/* copy from database to file */\n\t\tEndCopyTo(cstate);\n\t}\n\n\tif (rel != NULL)\n\t\ttable_close(rel, NoLock);\n}\n\n/*\n * Extract a CopyHeaderChoice value from a DefElem.  This is like\n * defGetBoolean() but also accepts the special value \"match\".\n */\nstatic CopyHeaderChoice\ndefGetCopyHeaderChoice(DefElem *def, bool is_from)\n{\n\t/*\n\t * If no parameter value given, assume \"true\" is meant.\n\t */\n\tif (def->arg == NULL)\n\t\treturn COPY_HEADER_TRUE;\n\n\t/*\n\t * Allow 0, 1, \"true\", \"false\", \"on\", \"off\", or \"match\".\n\t */\n\tswitch (nodeTag(def->arg))\n\t{\n\t\tcase T_Integer:\n\t\t\tswitch (intVal(def->arg))\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\tcase 0:\n\t\t\t\t\treturn COPY_HEADER_FALSE;\n\t\t\t\tcase 1:\n\t\t\t\t\treturn COPY_HEADER_TRUE;\n\t\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\t\t/* otherwise, error out below */\n\t\t\t\t\tbreak;\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tbreak;\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\tchar\t   *sval = defGetString(def);\n\n\t\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t\t * The set of strings accepted here should match up with the\n\t\t\t\t * grammar's opt_boolean_or_string production.\n\t\t\t\t */\n\t\t\t\tif (pg_strcasecmp(sval, \"true\") == 0)\n\t\t\t\t\treturn COPY_HEADER_TRUE;\n\t\t\t\tif (pg_strcasecmp(sval, \"false\") == 0)\n\t\t\t\t\treturn COPY_HEADER_FALSE;\n\t\t\t\tif (pg_strcasecmp(sval, \"on\") == 0)\n\t\t\t\t\treturn COPY_HEADER_TRUE;\n\t\t\t\tif (pg_strcasecmp(sval, \"off\") == 0)\n\t\t\t\t\treturn COPY_HEADER_FALSE;\n\t\t\t\tif (pg_strcasecmp(sval, \"match\") == 0)\n\t\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t\tif (!is_from)\n\t\t\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_FEATURE_NOT_SUPPORTED),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"cannot use \\\"%s\\\" with HEADER in COPY TO\",\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tsval)));\n\t\t\t\t\treturn COPY_HEADER_MATCH;\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tbreak;\n\t}\n\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_SYNTAX_ERROR),\n\t\t\t errmsg(\"%s requires a Boolean value or \\\"match\\\"\",\n\t\t\t\t\tdef->defname)));\n\treturn COPY_HEADER_FALSE;\t/* keep compiler quiet */\n}\n\n/*\n * Extract a CopyOnErrorChoice value from a DefElem.\n */\nstatic CopyOnErrorChoice\ndefGetCopyOnErrorChoice(DefElem *def, ParseState *pstate, bool is_from)\n{\n\tchar\t   *sval = defGetString(def);\n\n\tif (!is_from)\n\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_INVALID_PARAMETER_VALUE),\n\t\t/*- translator: first %s is the name of a COPY option, e.g. ON_ERROR,\n\t\t second %s is a COPY with direction, e.g. COPY TO */\n\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"COPY %s cannot be used with %s\", \"ON_ERROR\", \"COPY TO\"),\n\t\t\t\t parser_errposition(pstate, def->location)));\n\n\t/*\n\t * Allow \"stop\", or \"ignore\" values.\n\t */\n\tif (pg_strcasecmp(sval, \"stop\") == 0)\n\t\treturn COPY_ON_ERROR_STOP;\n\tif (pg_strcasecmp(sval, \"ignore\") == 0)\n\t\treturn COPY_ON_ERROR_IGNORE;\n\n\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_INVALID_PARAMETER_VALUE),\n\t/*- translator: first %s is the name of a COPY option, e.g. ON_ERROR */\n\t\t\t errmsg(\"COPY %s \\\"%s\\\" not recognized\", \"ON_ERROR\", sval),\n\t\t\t parser_errposition(pstate, def->location)));\n\treturn COPY_ON_ERROR_STOP;\t/* keep compiler quiet */\n}\n\n/*\n * Extract REJECT_LIMIT value from a DefElem.\n *\n * REJECT_LIMIT can be specified in two ways: as an int64 for the COPY command\n * option or as a single-quoted string for the foreign table option using\n * file_fdw. Therefore this function needs to handle both formats.\n */\nstatic int64\ndefGetCopyRejectLimitOption(DefElem *def)\n{\n\tint64\t\treject_limit;\n\n\tif (def->arg == NULL)\n\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_SYNTAX_ERROR),\n\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"%s requires a numeric value\",\n\t\t\t\t\t\tdef->defname)));\n\telse if (nodeTag(def->arg) == T_String)\n\t\treject_limit = pg_strtoint64(strVal(def->arg));\n\telse\n\t\treject_limit = defGetInt64(def);\n\n\tif (reject_limit <= 0)\n\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_INVALID_PARAMETER_VALUE),\n\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"REJECT_LIMIT (%\" PRId64 \") must be greater than zero\",\n\t\t\t\t\t\treject_limit)));\n\n\treturn reject_limit;\n}\n\n/*\n * Extract a CopyLogVerbosityChoice value from a DefElem.\n */\nstatic CopyLogVerbosityChoice\ndefGetCopyLogVerbosityChoice(DefElem *def, ParseState *pstate)\n{\n\tchar\t   *sval;\n\n\t/*\n\t * Allow \"silent\", \"default\", or \"verbose\" values.\n\t */\n\tsval = defGetString(def);\n\tif (pg_strcasecmp(sval, \"silent\") == 0)\n\t\treturn COPY_LOG_VERBOSITY_SILENT;\n\tif (pg_strcasecmp(sval, \"default\") == 0)\n\t\treturn COPY_LOG_VERBOSITY_DEFAULT;\n\tif (pg_strcasecmp(sval, \"verbose\") == 0)\n\t\treturn COPY_LOG_VERBOSITY_VERBOSE;\n\n\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_INVALID_PARAMETER_VALUE),\n\t/*- translator: first %s is the name of a COPY option, e.g. ON_ERROR */\n\t\t\t errmsg(\"COPY %s \\\"%s\\\" not recognized\", \"LOG_VERBOSITY\", sval),\n\t\t\t parser_errposition(pstate, def->location)));\n\treturn COPY_LOG_VERBOSITY_DEFAULT;\t/* keep compiler quiet */\n}\n\n/*\n * Process the statement option list for COPY.\n *\n * Scan the options list (a list of DefElem) and transpose the information\n * into *opts_out, applying appropriate error checking.\n *\n * If 'opts_out' is not NULL, it is assumed to be filled with zeroes initially.\n *\n * This is exported so that external users of the COPY API can sanity-check\n * a list of options.  In that usage, 'opts_out' can be passed as NULL and\n * the collected data is just leaked until CurrentMemoryContext is reset.\n *\n * Note that additional checking, such as whether column names listed in FORCE\n * QUOTE actually exist, has to be applied later.  This just checks for\n * self-consistency of the options list.\n */\nvoid\nProcessCopyOptions(ParseState *pstate,\n\t\t\t\t   CopyFormatOptions *opts_out,\n\t\t\t\t   bool is_from,\n\t\t\t\t   List *options)\n{\n\tbool\t\tformat_specified = false;\n\tbool\t\tfreeze_specified = false;\n\tbool\t\theader_specified = false;\n\tbool\t\ton_error_specified = false;\n\tbool\t\tlog_verbosity_specified = false;\n\tbool\t\treject_limit_specified = false;\n\tListCell   *option;\n\n\t/* Support external use for option sanity checking */\n\tif (opts_out == NULL)\n\t\topts_out = (CopyFormatOptions *) palloc0(sizeof(CopyFormatOptions));\n\n\topts_out->file_encoding = -1;\n\n\t/* Extract options from the statement node tree */\n\tforeach(option, options)\n\t{\n\t\tDefElem    *defel = lfirst_node(DefElem, option);\n\n\t\tif (strcmp(defel->defname, \"format\") == 0)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tchar\t   *fmt = defGetString(defel);\n\n\t\t\tif (format_specified)\n\t\t\t\terrorConflictingDefElem(defel, pstate);\n\t\t\tformat_specified = true;\n\t\t\tif (strcmp(fmt, \"text\") == 0)\n\t\t\t\t /* default format */ ;\n\t\t\telse if (strcmp(fmt, \"csv\") == 0)\n\t\t\t\topts_out->csv_mode = true;\n\t\t\telse if (strcmp(fmt, \"binary\") == 0)\n\t\t\t\topts_out->binary = true;\n\t\t\telse\n\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_INVALID_PARAMETER_VALUE),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"COPY format \\\"%s\\\" not recognized\", fmt),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t parser_errposition(pstate, defel->location)));\n\t\t}\n\t\telse if (strcmp(defel->defname, \"freeze\") == 0)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tif (freeze_specified)\n\t\t\t\terrorConflictingDefElem(defel, pstate);\n\t\t\tfreeze_specified = true;\n\t\t\topts_out->freeze = defGetBoolean(defel);\n\t\t}\n\t\telse if (strcmp(defel->defname, \"delimiter\") == 0)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tif (opts_out->delim)\n\t\t\t\terrorConflictingDefElem(defel, pstate);\n\t\t\topts_out->delim = defGetString(defel);\n\t\t}\n\t\telse if (strcmp(defel->defname, \"null\") == 0)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tif (opts_out->null_print)\n\t\t\t\terrorConflictingDefElem(defel, pstate);\n\t\t\topts_out->null_print = defGetString(defel);\n\t\t}\n\t\telse if (strcmp(defel->defname, \"default\") == 0)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tif (opts_out->default_print)\n\t\t\t\terrorConflictingDefElem(defel, pstate);\n\t\t\topts_out->default_print = defGetString(defel);\n\t\t}\n\t\telse if (strcmp(defel->defname, \"header\") == 0)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tif (header_specified)\n\t\t\t\terrorConflictingDefElem(defel, pstate);\n\t\t\theader_specified = true;\n\t\t\topts_out->header_line = defGetCopyHeaderChoice(defel, is_from);\n\t\t}\n\t\telse if (strcmp(defel->defname, \"quote\") == 0)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tif (opts_out->quote)\n\t\t\t\terrorConflictingDefElem(defel, pstate);\n\t\t\topts_out->quote = defGetString(defel);\n\t\t}\n\t\telse if (strcmp(defel->defname, \"escape\") == 0)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tif (opts_out->escape)\n\t\t\t\terrorConflictingDefElem(defel, pstate);\n\t\t\topts_out->escape = defGetString(defel);\n\t\t}\n\t\telse if (strcmp(defel->defname, \"force_quote\") == 0)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tif (opts_out->force_quote || opts_out->force_quote_all)\n\t\t\t\terrorConflictingDefElem(defel, pstate);\n\t\t\tif (defel->arg && IsA(defel->arg, A_Star))\n\t\t\t\topts_out->force_quote_all = true;\n\t\t\telse if (defel->arg && IsA(defel->arg, List))\n\t\t\t\topts_out->force_quote = castNode(List, defel->arg);\n\t\t\telse\n\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_INVALID_PARAMETER_VALUE),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"argument to option \\\"%s\\\" must be a list of column names\",\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tdefel->defname),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t parser_errposition(pstate, defel->location)));\n\t\t}\n\t\telse if (strcmp(defel->defname, \"force_not_null\") == 0)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tif names\",\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tdefel->defname),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t parser_errposition(pstate, defel->location)));\n\t\t}\n\t\telse if (strcmp(defel->defname, \"force_null\") == 0)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tif (opts_out->force_null || opts_out->force_null_all)\n\t\t\t\terrorConflictingDefElem(defel, pstate);\n\t\t\tif (defel->arg && IsA(defel->arg, A_Star))\n\t\t\t\topts_out->force_null_all = defel->arg);\n\t\t\telse\n\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_INVALID_PARAMETER_VALUE),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"argument to option \\\"%s\\\" must be a list of column names\",\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tdefel->defname),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t parser_errposition(pstate, defel->location)));\n\t\t}\n\t\telse if (strcmp(defel->defname, \"convert_selectively\") == It's\n\t\t\t * allowed for the column list to be NIL.\n\t\t\t */\n\t\t\tif (opts_out->convert_selectively)\n\t\t\t\terrorConflictingDefElem(defel, pstate);\n\t\t\topts_out->convert_selectively = (opts_out->file_encoding >= 0)\n\t\t\t\terrorConflictingDefElem(defel, pstate);\n\t\t\topts_out->file_encoding = pg_char_to_encoding(defGetString(defel));\n\t\t\tif (opts_out->file_encoding < 0)\n\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_INVALID_PARAMETER_VALUE),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"argument to option \\\"%s\\\" must be a valid encoding (strcmp(defel->defname, \"log_verbosity\") == 0)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tif (log_verbosity_specified)\n\t\t\t\terrorConflictingDefElem(defel, pstate);\n\t\t\tlog_verbosity_specified = defGetCopyRejectLimitOption(defel);\n\t\t}\n\t\telse\n\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_SYNTAX_ERROR),\n\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"option \\\"%s\\\" not transaction\")));\n\t\t\t\t\t/* Validate message type and set packet size limit */\n\t\t\t\t\tswitch (mtype)\n\t\t\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t\t\tcase PqMsg_CopyData:\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tmaxmsglen = PQ_LARGE_MESSAGE_LIMIT;\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tbreak;\n\t\t\t\t\t\tcase PqMsg_CopyDone:\n\t\t\t\t\t\tcase PqMsg_CopyFail:\n\t\t\t\t\t\tcase PqMsg_Flush:\n\t\t\t\t\t\tcase PqMsg_Sync:\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tmaxmsglen = PQ_SMALL_MESSAGE_LIMIT;\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tbreak;\n\t\t\t\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_PROTOCOL_VIOLATION),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"unexpected message type 0x%02X during COPY from stdin\",\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tmtype)));\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tmaxmsglen = 0;\t/* keep compiler quiet */\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tbreak;\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\t/* Now collect the message body */\n\t\t\t\t\tif (pq_getmessage(cstate->fe_msgbuf, maxmsglen))\n\t\t\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_CONNECTION_FAILURE),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"unexpected EOF on client connection with an open transaction\")));\n\t\t\t\t\tRESUME_CANCEL_INTERRUPTS();\n\t\t\t\t\t/* ... and process it */\n\t\t\t\t\tswitch (mtype)\n\t\t\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t\t\tcase PqMsg_CopyData:\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tbreak;\n\t\t\t\t\t\tcase PqMsg_CopyDone:\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t/* COPY IN correctly terminated by frontend */\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tcstate->raw_reached_eof = true;\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\treturn bytesread;\n\t\t\t\t\t\tcase PqMsg_CopyFail:\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_QUERY_CANCELED),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"COPY from stdin failed: %s\",\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tpq_getmsgstring(cstate->fe_msgbuf))));\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tbreak;\n\t\t\t\t\t\tcase PqMsg_Flush:\n\t\t\t\t\t\tcase PqMsg_Sync:\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t * Ignore Flush/Sync for the convenience of client\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t * libraries (such as libpq) that may send those\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t * without noticing that the command they just\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t * sent was COPY.\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t */\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tgoto readmessage;\n\t\t\t\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tAssert(false);\t/* NOT REACHED */\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tavail = cstate->fe_msgbuf->len - cstate->fe_msgbuf->cursor;\n\t\t\t\tif (avail > maxread)\n\t\t\t\t\tavail = maxread;\n\t\t\t\tpq_copymsgbytes(cstate->fe_msgbuf, databuf, avail);\n\t\t\t\tdatabuf = (void *) ((char *) databuf + avail);\n\t\t\t\tmaxread -= avail;\n\t\t\t\tbytesread += avail;\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tbreak;\n\t\tcase COPY_CALLBACK:\n\t\t\tbytesread = cstate->data_source_cb(databuf, minread, maxread);\n\t\t\tbreak;\n\t}\n\n\treturn bytesread;\n}\n\n\n/*\n * These functions do apply some data conversion\n */\n\n/*\n * CopyGetInt32 reads an int32 that appears in network byte order\n *\n * Returns true if OK, false if EOF\n */\nstatic inline bool\nCopyGetInt32(CopyFromState cstate, int32 *val)\n{\n\tuint32\t\tbuf;\n\n\tif (CopyReadBinaryData(cstate, (char *) &buf, sizeof(buf)) != sizeof(buf))\n\t{\n\t\t*val = 0;\t\t\t\t/* suppress compiler warning */\n\t\treturn false;\n\t}\n\t*val = (int32) pg_ntoh32(buf);\n\treturn true;\n}\n\n/*\n * CopyGetInt16 reads an int16 that appears in network byte order\n */\nstatic inline bool\nCopyGetInt16(CopyFromState cstate, int16 *val)\n{\n\tuint16\t\tbuf;\n\n\tif (CopyReadBinaryData(cstate, (char *) &buf, sizeof(buf)) != sizeof(buf))\n\t{\n\t\t*val = 0;\t\t\t\t/* suppress compiler warning */\n\t\treturn false;\n\t}\n\t*val = (int16) pg_ntoh16(buf);\n\treturn true;\n}\n\n\n/*\n * Perform encoding conversion on data in 'raw_buf', writing the converted\n * data into 'input_buf'.\n *\n * On entry, there must be some data to convert in 'raw_buf'.\n */\nstatic void\nCopyConvertBuf(CopyFromState cstate)\n{\n\t/*\n\t * If the file and server encoding are the same, no encoding conversion is\n\t * required.  However, we still need to verify that the input is valid for\n\t * the encoding.\n\t */\n\tif (!cstate->need_transcoding)\n\t{\n\t\t/*\n\t\t * When conversion is not required, input_buf and raw_buf are the\n\t\t * same.  raw_buf_len is the total number of bytes in the buffer, and\n\t\t * input_buf_len tracks how many of those bytes have already been\n\t\t * verified.\n\t\t */\n\t\tint\t\t\tpreverifiedlen = cstate->input_buf_len;\n\t\tint\t\t\tunverifiedlen = cstate->raw_buf_len - cstate->input_buf_len;\n\t\tint\t\t\tnverified;\n\n\t\tif (unverifiedlen == 0)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t * If no more raw data is coming, report the EOF to the caller.\n\t\t\t */\n\t\t\tif (cstate->raw_reached_eof)\n\t\t\t\tcstate->input_reached_eof = true;\n\t\t\treturn;\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t/*\n\t\t * Verify the new data, including any residual unverified bytes from\n\t\t * previous round.\n\t\t */\n\t\tnverified = pg_encoding_verifymbstr(cstate->file_encoding,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tcstate->raw_buf + preverifiedlen,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tunverifiedlen);\n\t\tif (nverified == 0)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t * Could not verify anything.\n\t\t\t *\n\t\t\t * If there is no more raw input data coming, it means that there\n\t\t\t * was an incomplete multi-byte sequence at the end.  Also, if\n\t\t\t * there's \"enough\" input left, we should be able to verify at\n\t\t\t * least one character, and a failure to do so means that we've\n\t\t\t * hit an invalid byte sequence.\n\t\t\t */\n\t\t\tif (cstate->raw_reached_eof || unverifiedlen >= pg_encoding_max_length(cstate->file_encoding))\n\t\t\t\tcstate->input_reached_error = true;\n\t\t\treturn;\n\t\t}\n\t\tcstate->input_buf_len += nverified;\n\t}\n\telse\n\t{\n\t\t/*\n\t\t * Encoding conversion is needed.\n\t\t */\n\t\tint\t\t\tnbytes;\n\t\tunsigned char *src;\n\t\tint\t\t\tsrclen;\n\t\tunsigned char *dst;\n\t\tint\t\t\tdstlen;\n\t\tint\t\t\tconvertedlen;\n\n\t\tif (RAW_BUF_BYTES(cstate) == 0)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t * If no more raw data is coming, report the EOF to the caller.\n\t\t\t */\n\t\t\tif (cstate->raw_reached_eof)\n\t\t\t\tcstate->input_reached_eof = true;\n\t\t\treturn;\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t/*\n\t\t * First, copy down any unprocessed data.\n\t\t */\n\t\tnbytes = INPUT_BUF_BYTES(cstate);\n\t\tif (nbytes > 0 && cstate->input_buf_index > 0)\n\t\t\tmemmove(cstate->input_buf, cstate->input_buf + cstate->input_buf_index,\n\t\t\t\t\tnbytes);\n\t\tcstate->input_buf_index = 0;\n\t\tcstate->input_buf_len = nbytes;\n\t\tcstate->input_buf[nbytes] = '\\0';\n\n\t\tsrc = (unsigned char *) cstate->raw_buf + cstate->raw_buf_index;\n\t\tsrclen = cstate->raw_buf_len - cstate->raw_buf_index;\n\t\tdst = (unsigned char *) cstate->input_buf + cstate->input_buf_len;\n\t\tdstlen = INPUT_BUF_SIZE - cstate->input_buf_len + 1;\n\n\t\t/*\n\t\t * Do the conversion.  This might stop short, if there is an invalid\n\t\t * byte sequence in the input.  We'll convert as much as we can in\n\t\t * that case.\n\t\t *\n\t\t * Note: Even if we hit an invalid byte sequence, we don't report the\n\t\t * error until all the valid bytes have been consumed.  The input\n\t\t * might contain an end-of-input marker (\\.), and we don't want to\n\t\t * report an error if the invalid byte sequence is after the\n\t\t * end-of-input marker.  We might unnecessarily convert some data\n\t\t * after the end-of-input marker as long as it's valid for the\n\t\t * encoding, but that's harmless.\n\t\t */\n\t\tconvertedlen = pg_do_encoding_conversion_buf(cstate->conversion_proc,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t cstate->file_encoding,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t GetDatabaseEncoding(),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t src, srclen,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t dst, dstlen,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t true);\n\t\tif (convertedlen == 0)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t * Could not convert anything.  If there is no more raw input data\n\t\t\t * coming, it means that there was an incomplete multi-byte\n\t\t\t * sequence at the end.  Also, if there is plenty of input left,\n\t\t\t * we should be able to convert at least one character, so a\n\t\t\t * failure to do so must mean that we've hit a byte sequence\n\t\t\t * that's invalid.\n\t\t\t */\n\t\t\tif (cstate->raw_reached_eof || srclen >= MAX_CONVERSION_INPUT_LENGTH)\n\t\t\t\tcstate->input_reached_error = true;\n\t\t\treturn;\n\t\t}\n\t\tcstate->raw_buf_index += convertedlen;\n\t\tcstate->input_buf_len += strlen((char *) dst);\n\t}\n}\n\n/*\n * Report an encoding or conversion error.\n */\nstatic void\nCopyConversionError(CopyFromState cstate)\n{\n\tAssert(cstate->raw_buf_len > 0);\n\tAssert(cstate->input_reached_error);\n\n\tif (!cstate->need_transcoding)\n\t{\n\t\t/*\n\t\t * Everything up to input_buf_len was successfully verified, and\n\t\t * input_buf_len points to the invalid or incomplete character.\n\t\t */\n\t\treport_invalid_encoding(cstate->file_encoding,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tcstate->raw_buf + cstate->input_buf_len,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tcstate->raw_buf_len - cstate->input_buf_len);\n\t}\n\telse\n\t{\n\t\t/*\n\t\t * raw_buf_index points to the invalid or untranslatable character. We\n\t\t * let the conversion routine report the error, because it can provide\n\t\t * a more specific error message than we could here.  An earlier call\n\t\t * to the conversion routine in CopyConvertBuf() detected that there\n\t\t * is an error, now we call the conversion routine again with\n\t\t * noError=false, to have it throw the error.\n\t\t */\n\t\tunsigned char *src;\n\t\tint\t\t\tsrclen;\n\t\tunsigned char *dst;\n\t\tint\t\t\tdstlen;\n\n\t\tsrc = (unsigned char *) cstate->raw_buf + cstate->raw_buf_index;\n\t\tsrclen = cstate->raw_buf_len - cstate->raw_buf_index;\n\t\tdst = (unsigned char *) cstate->input_buf + cstate->input_buf_len;\n\t\tdstlen = INPUT_BUF_SIZE - cstate->input_buf_len + 1;\n\n\t\t(void) pg_do_encoding_conversion_buf(cstate->conversion_proc,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t cstate->file_encoding,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t GetDatabaseEncoding(),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t src, srclen,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t dst, dstlen,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t false);\n\n\t\t/*\n\t\t * The conversion routine should have reported an error, so this\n\t\t * should not be reached.\n\t\t */\n\t\telog(ERROR, \"encoding conversion failed without error\");\n\t}\n}\n\n/*\n * Load more data from data source to raw_buf.\n *\n * If RAW_BUF_BYTES(cstate) > 0, the unprocessed bytes are moved to the\n * beginning of the buffer, and we load new data after that.\n */\nstatic void\nCopyLoadRawBuf(CopyFromState cstate)\n{\n\tint\t\t\tnbytes;\n\tint\t\t\tinbytes;\n\n\t/*\n\t * In text mode, if encoding conversion is not required, raw_buf and\n\t * input_buf point to the same buffer.  Their len/index better agree, too.\n\t */\n\tif (cstate->raw_buf == cstate->input_buf)\n\t{\n\t\tAssert(!cstate->need_transcoding);\n\t\tAssert(cstate->raw_buf_index == cstate->input_buf_index);\n\t\tAssert(cstate->input_buf_len <= cstate->raw_buf_len);\n\t}\n\n\t/*\n\t * Copy down the unprocessed data if any.\n\t */\n\tnbytes = RAW_BUF_BYTES(cstate);\n\tif (nbytes > 0 && cstate->raw_buf_index > 0)\n\t\tmemmove(cstate->raw_buf, cstate->raw_buf + cstate->raw_buf_index,\n\t\t\t\tnbytes);\n\tcstate->raw_buf_len -= cstate->raw_buf_index;\n\tcstate->raw_buf_index = 0;\n\n\t/*\n\t * If raw_buf and input_buf are in fact the same buffer, adjust the\n\t * input_buf variables, too.\n\t */\n\tif (cstate->raw_buf == cstate->input_buf)\n\t{\n\t\tcstate->input_buf_len -= cstate->input_buf_index;\n\t\tcstate->input_buf_index = 0;\n\t}\n\n\t/* Load more data */\n\tinbytes = CopyGetData(cstate, cstate->raw_buf + cstate->raw_buf_len,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t  1, RAW_BUF_SIZE - cstate->raw_buf_len);\n\tnbytes += inbytes;\n\tcstate->raw_buf[nbytes] = '\\0';\n\tcstate->raw_buf_len = nbytes;\n\n\tcstate->bytes_processed += inbytes;\n\tpgstat_progress_update_param(PROGRESS_COPY_BYTES_PROCESSED, cstate->bytes_processed);\n\n\tif (inbytes == 0)\n\t\tcstate->raw_reached_eof = true;\n}\n\n/*\n * CopyLoadInputBuf loads some more data into input_buf\n *\n * On return, at least one more input character is loaded into\n * input_buf, or input_reached_eof is set.\n *\n * If INPUT_BUF_BYTES(cstate) > 0, the unprocessed bytes are moved to the start\n * of the buffer and then we load more data after that.\n */\nstatic void\nCopyLoadInputBuf(CopyFromState cstate)\n{\n\tint\t\t\tnbytes = INPUT_BUF_BYTES(cstate);\n\n\t/*\n\t * The caller has updated input_buf_index to indicate how much of the\n\t * input has been consumed and isn't needed anymore.  If input_buf is the\n\t * same physical area as raw_buf, update raw_buf_index accordingly.\n\t */\n\tif (cstate->raw_buf == cstate->input_buf)\n\t{\n\t\tAssert(!cstate->need_transcoding);\n\t\tAssert(cstate->input_buf_index >= cstate->raw_buf_index);\n\t\tcstate->raw_buf_index = cstate->input_buf_index;\n\t}\n\n\tfor (;;)\n\t{\n\t\t/* If we now have some unconverted data, try to convert it */\n\t\tCopyConvertBuf(cstate);\n\n\t\t/* If we now have some more input bytes ready, return them */\n\t\tif (INPUT_BUF_BYTES(cstate) > nbytes)\n\t\t\treturn;\n\n\t\t/*\n\t\t * If we reached an invalid byte sequence, or we're at an incomplete\n\t\t * multi-byte character but there is no more raw input data, report\n\t\t * conversion error.\n\t\t */\n\t\tif (cstate->input_reached_error)\n\t\t\tCopyConversionError(cstate);\n\n\t\t/* no more input, and everything has been converted */\n\t\tif (cstate->input_reached_eof)\n\t\t\tbreak;\n\n\t\t/* Try to load more raw data */\n\t\tAssert(!cstate->raw_reached_eof);\n\t\tCopyLoadRawBuf(cstate);\n\t}\n}\n\n/*\n * CopyReadBinaryData\n *\n * Reads up to 'nbytes' bytes from cstate->copy_file via cstate->raw_buf\n * and writes them to 'dest'.  Returns the number of bytes read (which\n * would be less than 'nbytes' only if we reach EOF).\n */\nstatic int\nCopyReadBinaryData(CopyFromState cstate, char *dest, int nbytes)\n{\n\tint\t\t\tcopied_bytes = 0;\n\n\tif (RAW_BUF_BYTES(cstate) >= nbytes)\n\t{\n\t\t/* Enough bytes are present in the buffer. */\n\t\tmemcpy(dest, cstate->raw_buf + cstate->raw_buf_index, nbytes);\n\t\tcstate->raw_buf_index += nbytes;\n\t\tcopied_bytes = nbytes;\n\t}\n\telse\n\t{\n\t\t/*\n\t\t * Not enough bytes in the buffer, so must read from the file.  Need\n\t\t * to loop since 'nbytes' could be larger than the buffer size.\n\t\t */\n\t\tdo\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tint\t\t\tcopy_bytes;\n\n\t\t\t/* Load more data if buffer is empty. */\n\t\t\tif (RAW_BUF_BYTES(cstate) == 0)\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\tCopyLoadRawBuf(cstate);\n\t\t\t\tif (cstate->raw_reached_eof)\n\t\t\t\t\tbreak;\t\t/* EOF */\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t/* Transfer some bytes. */\n\t\t\tcopy_bytes = Min(nbytes - copied_bytes, RAW_BUF_BYTES(cstate));\n\t\t\tmemcpy(dest, cstate->raw_buf + cstate->raw_buf_index, copy_bytes);\n\t\t\tcstate->raw_buf_index += copy_bytes;\n\t\t\tdest += copy_bytes;\n\t\t\tcopied_bytes += copy_bytes;\n\t\t} while (copied_bytes < nbytes);\n\t}\n\n\treturn copied_bytes;\n}\n\n/*\n * This function is exposed for use by extensions that read raw fields in the\n * next line. See NextCopyFromRawFieldsInternal() for details.\n */\nbool\nNextCopyFromRawFields(CopyFromState cstate, char ***fields, int *nfields)\n{\n\treturn NextCopyFromRawFieldsInternal(cstate, fields, nfields,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t cstate->opts.csv_mode);\n}\n\n/*\n * Workhorse for NextCopyFromRawFields().\n *\n * Read raw fields in the next line for COPY FROM in text or csv mode. Return\n * false if no more lines.\n *\n * An internal temporary buffer is returned via 'fields'. It is valid until\n * the next call of the function. Since the function returns all raw fields\n * in the input file, 'nfields' could be different from the number of columns\n * in the relation.\n *\n * NOTE: force_not_null option are not applied to the returned fields.\n *\n * We use pg_attribute_always_inline to reduce function call overhead\n * and to help compilers to optimize away the 'is_csv' condition when called\n * by internal functions such as CopyFromTextLikeOneRow().\n */\nstatic pg_attribute_always_inline bool\nNextCopyFromRawFieldsInternal(CopyFromState cstate, char ***fields, int *nfields, bool is_csv)\n{\n\tint\t\t\tfldct;\n\tbool\t\tdone;\n\n\t/* only available for text or csv input */\n\tAssert(!cstate->opts.binary);\n\n\t/* on input check that the header line is correct if needed */\n\tif (cstate->cur_lineno == 0 && cstate->opts.header_line)\n\t{\n\t\tListCell   *cur;\n\t\tTupleDesc\ttupDesc;\n\n\t\ttupDesc = RelationGetDescr(cstate->rel);\n\n\t\tcstate->cur_lineno++;\n\t\tdone = CopyReadLine(cstate, is_csv);\n\n\t\tif (cstate->opts.header_line == COPY_HEADER_MATCH)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tint\t\t\tfldnum;\n\n\t\t\tif (is_csv)\n\t\t\t\tfldct = CopyReadAttributesCSV(cstate);\n\t\t\telse\n\t\t\t\tfldct = CopyReadAttributesText(cstate);\n\n\t\t\tif (fldct != list_length(cstate->attnumlist))\n\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_BAD_COPY_FILE_FORMAT),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"wrong number of fields in header line: got %d, expected %d\",\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tfldct, list_length(cstate->attnumlist))));\n\n\t\t\tfldnum = 0;\n\t\t\tforeach(cur, cstate->attnumlist)\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\tint\t\t\tattnum = lfirst_int(cur);\n\t\t\t\tchar\t   *colName;\n\t\t\t\tForm_pg_attribute attr = TupleDescAttr(tupDesc, attnum - 1);\n\n\t\t\t\tAssert(fldnum < cstate->max_fields);\n\n\t\t\t\tcolName = cstate->raw_fields[fldnum++];\n\t\t\t\tif (colName == NULL)\n\t\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_BAD_COPY_FILE_FORMAT),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"column name mismatch in header line field %d: got null value (\\\"%s\\\"), expected \\\"%s\\\"\",\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tfldnum, cstate->opts.null_print, NameStr(attr->attname))));\n\n\t\t\t\tif (pg_strcasecmp(NameStr(attr->attname), colName) != 0)\n\t\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_BAD_COPY_FILE_FORMAT),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"column name mismatch in header line field %d: got \\\"%s\\\", expected \\\"%s\\\"\",\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tfldnum, colName, NameStr(attr->attname))));\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif (done)\n\t\t\treturn false;\n\t}\n\n\tcstate->cur_lineno++;\n\n\t/* Actually read the line into memory here */\n\tdone = CopyReadLine(cstate, is_csv);\n\n\t/*\n\t * EOF at start of line means we're done.  If we see EOF after some\n\t * characters, we act as though it was newline followed by EOF, ie,\n\t * process the line and then exit loop on next iteration.\n\t */\n\tif (done && cstate->line_buf.len == 0)\n\t\treturn false;\n\n\t/* Parse the line into de-escaped field values */\n\tif (is_csv)\n\t\tfldct = CopyReadAttributesCSV(cstate);\n\telse\n\t\tfldct = CopyReadAttributesText(cstate);\n\n\t*fields = cstate->raw_fields;\n\t*nfields = fldct;\n\treturn true;\n}\n\n/*\n * Read next tuple from file for COPY FROM. Return false if no more tuples.\n *\n * 'econtext' is used to evaluate default expression for each column that is\n * either not read from the file or is using the DEFAULT option of COPY FROM.\n * It can be NULL when no default values are used, i.e. when all columns are\n * read from the file, and DEFAULT option is unset.\n *\n * 'values' and 'nulls' arrays must be the same length as columns of the\n * relation passed to BeginCopyFrom. This function fills the arrays.\n */\nbool\nNextCopyFrom(CopyFromState cstate, ExprContext *econtext,\n\t\t\t Datum *values, bool *nulls)\n{\n\tTupleDesc\ttupDesc;\n\tAttrNumber\tnum_phys_attrs,\n\t\t\t\tnum_defaults = cstate->num_defaults;\n\tint\t\t\ti;\n\tint\t\t   *defmap = cstate->defmap;\n\tExprState **defexprs = cstate->defexprs;\n\n\ttupDesc = RelationGetDescr(cstate->rel);\n\tnum_phys_attrs = tupDesc->natts;\n\n\t/* Initialize all values for row to NULL */\n\tMemSet(values, 0, num_phys_attrs * sizeof(Datum));\n\tMemSet(nulls, true, num_phys_attrs * sizeof(bool));\n\tMemSet(cstate->defaults, false, num_phys_attrs * sizeof(bool));\n\n\t/* Get one row from source */\n\tif (!cstate->routine->CopyFromOneRow(cstate, econtext, values, nulls))\n\t\treturn false;\n\n\t/*\n\t * Now compute and insert any defaults available for the columns not\n\t * provided by the input data.  Anything not processed here or above will\n\t * remain NULL.\n\t */\n\tfor (i = 0; i < num_defaults; i++)\n\t{\n\t\t/*\n\t\t * The caller must supply econtext and have switched into the\n\t\t * ExecEvalExpr(defexprs[defmap[i]], econtext,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t &nulls[defmap[i]]);\n\t}\n\n\treturn true;\n}\n\n/* Implementation of the per-row callback for text format */\nbool\nCopyFromTextOneRow(CopyFromState cstate, ExprContext *econtext, Datum *values,\n\t\t\t\t   bool *nulls)\n{\n\treturn CopyFromTextLikeOneRow(cstate, econtext, values, nulls, false);\n}\n\n/* Implementation of the per-row callback for CSV format */\nbool\nCopyFromCSVOneRow(CopyFromState cstate, ExprContext *econtext, Datum *values,\n\t\t\t\t  bool *nulls)\n{\n\treturn CopyFromTextLikeOneRow(cstate, econtext, values, nulls, true);\n}\n\n/*\n * Workhorse for CopyFromTextOneRow() and CopyFromCSVOneRow().\n *\n * We use pg_attribute_always_inline to reduce function call overhead\n * and to help compilers to optimize away the 'is_csv' condition.\n */\nstatic pg_attribute_always_inline bool\nCopyFromTextLikeOneRow(CopyFromState cstate, ExprContext *econtext,\n\t\t\t\t\t   Datum *values, bool *nulls, bool is_csv)\n{\n\tTupleDesc\ttupDesc;\n\tAttrNumber\tattr_count;\n\tFmgrInfo   *in_functions = cstate->in_functions;\n\tOid\t\t   *typioparams = cstate->typioparams;\n\tExprState **defexprs = cstate->defexprs;\n\tchar\t  **field_strings;\n\tListCell   *cur;\n\tint\t\t\tfldct;\n\tint\t\t\tfieldno;\n\tchar\t   *string;\n\n\ttupDesc = RelationGetDescr(cstate->rel);\n\tattr_count = list_length(cstate->attnumlist);\n\n\t/* read raw fields in the next line */\n\tif (!NextCopyFromRawFieldsInternal(cstate, &field_strings, &fldct, is_csv))\n\t\treturn false;\n\n\t/* check for overflowing fields */\n\tif (attr_count > 0 && fldct > attr_count)\n\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_BAD_COPY_FILE_FORMAT),\n\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"extra data after last expected column\")));\n\n\tfieldno = 0;\n\n\t/* Loop to read the user attributes on the line. */\n\tforeach(cur, cstate->attnumlist)\n\t{\n\t\tint\t\t\tattnum = lfirst_int(cur);\n\t\tint\t\t\tm = attnum - 1;\n\t\tForm_pg_attribute att = TupleDescAttr(tupDesc, m);\n\n\t\tif (fieldno >= field_strings[fieldno++];\n\n\t\tif (cstate->convert_select_flags &&\n\t\t\t!cstate->convert_select_flags[m])\n\t\t{\n\t\t\t/* ignore input field, leaving column as NULL */\n\t\t\tcontinue;\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif (is_csv)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tif (string == NULL &&\n\t\t\t\tcstate->opts.force_notnull_flags[m])\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t\t * FORCE_NOT_NULL option is set and column is NULL - convert\n\t\t\t\t * it to the NULL string.\n\t\t\t\t */\n\t\t\t\tstring = cstate->opts.null_print;\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\telse if (string != NULL && cstate->opts.force_null_flags[m]\n\t\t\t\t\t && strcmp(string, cstate->opts.null_print) == 0)\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t\t * FORCE_NULL option is set and column matches the NULL\n\t\t\t\t * string. It must have been quoted, or otherwise the string\n\t\t\t\t * would already have been set to NULL. NULL);\n\t\t\tAssert(CurrentMemoryContext == econtext->ecxt_per_tuple_memory);\n\n\t\t\tvalues[m] = ExecEvalExpr(defexprs[m], econtext, &nulls[m]);\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t/*\n\t\t * If ON_ERROR is specified with IGNORE, skip rows with soft errors\n\t\t */\n\t\telse if cstate->escontext,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t&values[m]))\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tAssert(cstate->opts.on_error != COPY_ON_ERROR_STOP);\n\n\t\t\tcstate->num_errors++;\n\n\t\t\tif (cstate->opts.log_verbosity == COPY_LOG_VERBOSITY_VERBOSE)\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t\t * Since we emit line number and column info in the below\n\t\t\t\t * notice message, we suppress error context information other\n\t\t\t\t * than the relation name.\n\t\t\t\t */\n\t\t\t\tAssert(!cstate->relname_only);\n\t\t\t\tcstate->relname_only = true;\n\n\t\t\t\tif (cstate->cur_attval)\n\t\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t\tchar\t   *attval;\n\n\t\t\t\t\tattval = CopyLimitPrintoutLength(cstate->cur_attval);\n\t\t\t\t\tereport(NOTICE,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\terrmsg(\"skipping row due to data type incompatibility at line %\" PRIu64 \" for column \\\"%s\\\": \\\"%s\\\"\",\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t   cstate->cur_lineno,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t   cstate->cur_attname,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t false;\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\treturn true;\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tcstate->cur_attname = NULL;\n\t\tcstate->cur_attval = NULL;\n\t}\n\n\tAssert(fieldno == attr_count);\n\n\treturn true;\n}\n\n/* Implementation of the per-row callback for binary format */\nbool\nCopyFromBinaryOneRow(CopyFromState cstate, ExprContext *econtext, Datum *values,\n\t\t\t\t\t bool *nulls)\n{\n\tTupleDesc\ttupDesc;\n\tAttrNumber\tattr_count;\n\tFmgrInfo   *in_functions = cstate->in_functions;\n\tOid\t\t   *typioparams = cstate->typioparams;\n\tint16\t\tfld_count;\n\tListCell   *cur;\n\n\ttupDesc = RelationGetDescr(cstate->rel);\n\tattr_count = list_length(cstate->attnumlist);\n\n\tcstate->cur_lineno++;\n\n\tif (!CopyGetInt16(cstate, &fld_count))\n\t{\n\t\t/* EOF detected (end of file, or protocol-level EOF) */\n\t\treturn false;\n\t}\n\n\tif (fld_count == -1)\n\t{\n\t\t/*\n\t\t * Received EOF marker.  Wait for the protocol-level EOF, and complain\n\t\t * if it doesn't come immediately.  In COPY FROM STDIN, this ensures\n\t\t * that we correctly handle CopyFail, if client chooses to send that\n\t\t * now.  When copying from file, we could ignore the rest of the file\n\t\t * like in text mode, but we choose to be consistent with the COPY\n\t\t * FROM STDIN case.\n\t\t */\n\t\tchar\t\tdummy;\n\n\t\tif (CopyReadBinaryData(cstate, &dummy, 1) > 0)\n\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_BAD_COPY_FILE_FORMAT),\n\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"received copy data after EOF marker\")));\n\t\treturn false;\n\t}\n\n\tif (fld_count != attr_count)\n\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_BAD_COPY_FILE_FORMAT),\n\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"row field count is %d, expected %d\",\n\t\t\t\t\t\t(int) fld_count, attr_count)));\n\n\tforeach(cur, cstate->attnumlist)\n\t{\n\t\tint\t\t\tattnum = lfirst_int(cur);\n\t\tint\t\t\tm = attnum - 1;\n\t\tForm_pg_attribute att = TupleDescAttr(tupDesc, m);\n\n\t\tcstate->cur_attname = NameStr(att->attname);\n\t\tvalues[m] = CopyReadBinaryAttribute(cstate,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t&in_functions[m],\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\ttypioparams[m],\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tatt->atttypmod,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t&nulls[m]);\n\t\tcstate->cur_attname = NULL;\n\t}\n\n\treturn true;\n}\n\n/*\n * Read the next input line and stash it in line_buf.\n *\n * Result is true if read was terminated by EOF, false if terminated\n * by newline.  The terminating newline or EOF marker is not included\n * in the final value of line_buf.\n */\nstatic bool\nCopyReadLine(CopyFromState cstate, bool is_csv)\n{\n\tbool\t\tresult;\n\n\tresetStringInfo(&cstate->line_buf);\n\tcstate->line_buf_valid = false;\n\n\t/* Parse data and transfer into line_buf */\n\tresult = CopyReadLineText(cstate, is_csv);\n\n\tif (result)\n\t{\n\t\t/*\n\t\t * Reached EOF.  In protocol version 3, we should ignore anything\n\t\t * after \\. up to the protocol end of copy data.  (XXX maybe better\n\t\t * not to treat \\. as special?)\n\t\t */\n\t\tif (cstate->copy_src == COPY_FRONTEND)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tint\t\t\tinbytes;\n\n\t\t\tdo\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\tinbytes = CopyGetData(cstate, cstate->input_buf,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t  1, INPUT_BUF_SIZE);\n\t\t\t} while (inbytes > 0);\n\t\t\tcstate->input_buf_index = 0;\n\t\t\tcstate->input_buf_len = 0;\n\t\t\tcstate->raw_buf_index = 0;\n\t\t\tcstate->raw_buf_len = 0;\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\telse\n\t{\n\t\t/*\n\t\t * If we didn't hit EOF, then we must have transferred the EOL marker\n\t\t * to line_buf along with the data.  Get rid of it.\n\t\t */\n\t\tswitch (cstate->eol_type)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tcase EOL_NL:\n\t\t\t\tAssert(cstate->line_buf.len >= 1);\n\t\t\t\tAssert(cstate->line_buf.data[cstate->line_buf.len - 1] == '\\n');\n\t\t\t\tcstate->line_buf.len--;\n\t\t\t\tcstate->line_buf.data[cstate->line_buf.len] = '\\0';\n\t\t\t\tbreak;\n\t\t\tcase EOL_CR:\n\t\t\t\tAssert(cstate->line_buf.len >= 1);\n\t\t\t\tAssert(cstate->line_buf.data[cstate->line_buf.len - 1] == '\\r');\n\t\t\t\tcstate->line_buf.len--;\n\t\t\t\tcstate->line_buf.data[cstate->line_buf.len] = '\\0';\n\t\t\t\tbreak;\n\t\t\tcase EOL_CRNL:\n\t\t\t\tAssert(cstate->line_buf.len >= 2);\n\t\t\t\tAssert(cstate->line_buf.data[cstate->line_buf.len - 2] == '\\r');\n\t\t\t\tAssert(cstate->line_buf.data[cstate->line_buf.len - 1] == '\\n');\n\t\t\t\tcstate->line_buf.len -= 2;\n\t\t\t\tcstate->line_buf.data[cstate->line_buf.len] = '\\0';\n\t\t\t\tbreak;\n\t\t\tcase EOL_UNKNOWN:\n\t\t\t\t/* shouldn't get here */\n\t\t\t\tAssert(false);\n\t\t\t\tbreak;\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t/* Now it's safe to use the buffer in error messages */\n\tcstate->line_buf_valid = true;\n\n\treturn result;\n}\n\n/*\n * CopyReadLineText - inner loop of CopyReadLine for text mode\n */\nstatic bool\nCopyReadLineText(CopyFromState cstate, bool is_csv)\n{\n\tchar\t   *copy_input_buf;\n\tint\t\t\tinput_buf_ptr;\n\tint\t\t\tcopy_buf_len;\n\tbool\t\tneed_data = false;\n\tbool\t\thit_eof = false;\n\tbool\t\tresult = false;\n\n\t/* CSV variables */\n\tbool\t\tin_quote = false,\n\t\t\t\tlast_was_esc = false;\n\tchar\t\tquotec = '\\0';\n\tchar\t\tescapec = '\\0';\n\n\tif (is_csv)\n\t{\n\t\tquotec = cstate->opts.quote[0];\n\t\tescapec = cstate->opts.escape[0];\n\t\t/* ignore special escape processing if it's the same as quotec */\n\t\tif (quotec == escapec)\n\t\t\tescapec = '\\0';\n\t}\n\n\t/*\n\t * The objective of this loop is to transfer the entire next input line\n\t * into line_buf.  Hence, we only care for detecting newlines (\\r and/or\n\t * \\n) and the end-of-copy marker (\\.).\n\t *\n\t * In CSV mode, \\r and \\n inside a quoted field are just part of the data\n\t * value and are put in line_buf.  We keep just enough state to know if we\n\t * are currently in a quoted field or not.\n\t *\n\t * The input has already been converted to the database encoding.  All\n\t * supported server encodings have the property that all bytes in a\n\t * multi-byte sequence have the high bit set, so a multibyte character\n\t * cannot contain any newline or escape characters embedded in the\n\t * multibyte sequence.  Therefore, we can process the input byte-by-byte,\n\t * regardless of the encoding.\n\t *\n\t * For speed, we try to move data from input_buf to line_buf in chunks\n\t * rather than one character at a time.  input_buf_ptr points to the next\n\t * character to examine; any characters from input_buf_index to\n\t * input_buf_ptr have been determined to be part of the line, but not yet\n\t * transferred to line_buf.\n\t *\n\t * For a little extra speed within the loop, we copy input_buf and\n\t * input_buf_len into local variables.\n\t */\n\tcopy_input_buf = cstate->input_buf;\n\tinput_buf_ptr = cstate->input_buf_index;\n\tcopy_buf_len = cstate->input_buf_len;\n\n\tfor (;;)\n\t{\n\t\tint\t\t\tprev_raw_ptr;\n\t\tchar\t\tc;\n\n\t\t/*\n\t\t * Load more data if needed.\n\t\t *\n\t\t * TODO: We could just force four bytes of read-ahead and avoid the\n\t\t * many calls to IF_NEED_REFILL_AND_NOT_EOF_CONTINUE().  That was\n\t\t * unsafe with the old v2 COPY protocol, but we don't support that\n\t\t * anymore.\n\t\t */\n\t\tif (input_buf_ptr >= copy_buf_len || need_data)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tREFILL_LINEBUF;\n\n\t\t\tCopyLoadInputBuf(cstate);\n\t\t\t/* update our local variables */\n\t\t\thit_eof = cstate->input_reached_eof;\n\t\t\tinput_buf_ptr = cstate->input_buf_index;\n\t\t\tcopy_buf_len = cstate->input_buf_len;\n\n\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t * If we are completely out of data, break out of the loop,\n\t\t\t * reporting EOF.\n\t\t\t */\n\t\t\tif (INPUT_BUF_BYTES(cstate) <= 0)\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\tresult = true;\n\t\t\t\tbreak;\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tneed_data = false;\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t/* OK to fetch a character */\n\t\tprev_raw_ptr = input_buf_ptr;\n\t\tc = copy_input_buf[input_buf_ptr++];\n\n\t\tif (is_csv)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t * If character is '\\r', we may need to look ahead below.  Force\n\t\t\t * fetch of the next character if we don't already have it.  We\n\t\t\t * need to do this before changing CSV state, in case '\\r' is also\n\t\t\t * the quote or escape character.\n\t\t\t */\n\t\t\tif (c == '\\r')\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\tIF_NEED_REFILL_AND_NOT_EOF_CONTINUE(0);\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t * Dealing with quotes and escapes here is mildly tricky. If the\n\t\t\t * quote char is also the escape char, there's no problem - we\n\t\t\t * just use the char as a toggle. If they are different, we need\n\t\t\t * to ensure that we only take account of an escape inside a\n\t\t\t * quoted field and immediately preceding a quote char, and not\n\t\t\t * the second in an escape-escape sequence.\n\t\t\t */\n\t\t\tif (in_quote && c == escapec)\n\t\t\t\tlast_was_esc = !last_was_esc;\n\t\t\tif (c == quotec && !last_was_esc)\n\t\t\t\tin_quote = !in_quote;\n\t\t\tif (c != escapec)\n\t\t\t\tlast_was_esc = false;\n\n\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t * Updating the line count for embedded CR and/or LF chars is\n\t\t\t * necessarily a little fragile - this test is probably about the\n\t\t\t * best we can do.  (XXX it's arguable whether we should do this\n\t\t\t * at all --- is cur_lineno a physical or logical count?)\n\t\t\t */\n\t\t\tif (in_quote && c == (cstate->eol_type == EOL_NL ? '\\n' : '\\r'))\n\t\t\t\tcstate->cur_lineno++;\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t/* Process \\r */\n\t\tif (c == '\\r' && (!is_csv || !in_quote))\n\t\t{\n\t\t\t/* Check for \\r\\n on first line, _and_ handle \\r\\n. */\n\t\t\tif (cstate->eol_type == EOL_UNKNOWN ||\n\t\t\t\tcstate->eol_type == EOL_CRNL)\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t\t * If need more data, go back to loop top to load it.\n\t\t\t\t *\n\t\t\t\t * Note that if we are at EOF, c will wind up as '\\0' because\n\t\t\t\t * of the guaranteed pad of input_buf.\n\t\t\t\t */\n\t\t\t\tIF_NEED_REFILL_AND_NOT_EOF_CONTINUE(0);\n\n\t\t\t\t/* get next char */\n\t\t\t\tc = copy_input_buf[input_buf_ptr];\n\n\t\t\t\tif (c == '\\n')\n\t\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t\tinput_buf_ptr++;\t/* eat newline */\n\t\t\t\t\tcstate->eol_type = EOL_CRNL;\t/* in case not set yet */\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\telse\n\t\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t\t/* found \\r, but no \\n */\n\t\t\t\t\tif (cstate->eol_type == EOL_CRNL)\n\t\t\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_BAD_COPY_FILE_FORMAT),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t !is_csv ?\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"literal carriage return found in data\") :\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"unquoted carriage return found in data\"),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t !is_csv ?\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t errhint(\"Use \\\"\\\\r\\\" to represent carriage return.\") :\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t errhint(\"Use quoted CSV field to represent carriage return.\")));\n\n\t\t\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t\t\t * if we got here, it is the first line and we didn't find\n\t\t\t\t\t * \\n, so don't consume the peeked character\n\t\t\t\t\t */\n\t\t\t\t\tcstate->eol_type = EOL_CR;\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\telse if (cstate->eol_type == EOL_NL)\n\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_BAD_COPY_FILE_FORMAT),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t !is_csv ?\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"literal carriage return found in data\") :\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"unquoted carriage return found in data\"),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t !is_csv ?\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errhint(\"Use \\\"\\\\r\\\" to represent carriage return.\") :\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errhint(\"Use quoted CSV field to represent carriage return.\")));\n\t\t\t/* If reach here, we have found the line terminator */\n\t\t\tbreak;\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t/* Process \\n */\n\t\tif (c == '\\n' && (!is_csv || !in_quote))\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tif (cstate->eol_type == EOL_CR || cstate->eol_type == EOL_CRNL)\n\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_BAD_COPY_FILE_FORMAT),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t !is_csv ?\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"literal newline found in data\") :\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"unquoted newline found in data\"),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t !is_csv ?\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errhint(\"Use \\\"\\\\n\\\" to represent newline.\") :\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errhint(\"Use quoted CSV field to represent newline.\")));\n\t\t\tcstate->eol_type = EOL_NL;\t/* in case not set yet */\n\t\t\t/* If reach here, we have found the line terminator */\n\t\t\tbreak;\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t/*\n\t\t * Process backslash, except in CSV mode where backslash is a normal\n\t\t * character.\n\t\t */\n\t\tif (c == '\\\\' && !is_csv)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tchar\t\tc2;\n\n\t\t\tIF_NEED_REFILL_AND_NOT_EOF_CONTINUE(0);\n\t\t\tIF_NEED_REFILL_AND_EOF_BREAK(0);\n\n\t\t\t/* -----\n\t\t\t * get next character\n\t\t\t * Note: we do not '.')\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\tinput_buf_ptr++;\t/* consume the '.' */\n\t\t\t\tif (cstate->eol_type == EOL_CRNL)\n\t\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t\t/* Get the next character */\n\t\t\t\t\tIF_NEED_REFILL_AND_NOT_EOF_CONTINUE(0);\n\t\t\t\t\t/* if hit_eof, c2 will become '\\0' */\n\t\t\t\t\tc2 = copy_input_buf[input_buf_ptr++];\n\n\t\t\t\t\tif (c2 == '\\n')\n\t\t\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_BAD_COPY_FILE_FORMAT),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"end-of-copy marker does not match previous newline style\")));\n\t\t\t\t\telse if (c2 != '\\r')\n\t\t\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_BAD_COPY_FILE_FORMAT),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"end-of-copy marker is not alone on its line\")));\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\t/* Get the next character */\n\t\t\t\tIF_NEED_REFILL_AND_NOT_EOF_CONTINUE(0);\n\t\t\t\t/* if hit_eof, c2 will become '\\0' */\n\t\t\t\tc2 = copy_input_buf[input_buf_ptr++];\n\n\t\t\t\tif (c2 != '\\r' && c2 != '\\n')\n\t\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_BAD_COPY_FILE_FORMAT),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"end-of-copy marker is not alone on its line\")));\n\n\t\t\t\tif ((cstate->eol_type == EOL_NL && c2 != '\\n') ||\n\t\t\t\t\t(cstate->eol_type == EOL_CRNL && c2 != '\\n') ||\n\t\t\t\t\t(cstate->eol_type == EOL_CR && c2 != '\\r'))\n\t\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_BAD_COPY_FILE_FORMAT),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"end-of-copy marker does not match previous newline style\")));\n\n\t\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t\t * If there is any data on this line before the \\., complain.\n\t\t\t\t */\n\t\t\t\tif (cstate->line_buf.len > 0 ||\n\t\t\t\t\tprev_raw_ptr > cstate->input_buf_index)\n\t\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_BAD_COPY_FILE_FORMAT),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"end-of-copy marker is not alone on its line\")));\n\n\t\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t\t * Discard the \\. and newline, then report EOF.\n\t\t\t\t */\n\t\t\t\tcstate->input_buf_index = input_buf_ptr;\n\t\t\t\tresult = true;\t/* report EOF */\n\t\t\t\tbreak;\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\telse\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t\t * If we are here, it means we found a backslash followed by\n\t\t\t\t * something other than a period. Note that this is compared to\n * the pre-de-escaped input string.\n *\n * The return value is the number of fields actually read.\n */\nstatic int\nCopyReadAttributesText(CopyFromState cstate)\n{\n\tchar\t\tdelimc = cstate->opts.delim[0];\n\tint\t\t\tfieldno;\n\tchar\t   *output_ptr;\n\tchar\t   *cur_ptr;\n\tchar\t   *line_end_ptr;\n\n\t/*\n\t * We need a special case for zero-column tables: check that the input\n\t * line is empty, and return.\n\t */\n\tif (cstate->max_fields <= 0)\n\t{\n\t\tif (cstate->line_buf.len != 0)\n\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_BAD_COPY_FILE_FORMAT),\n\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"extra data after last expected column\")));\n\t\treturn 0;\n\t}\n\n\tresetStringInfo(&cstate->attribute_buf);\n\n\t/*\n\t * The de-escaped attributes will certainly not be longer than the input\n\t * data line, so we can just force attribute_buf to be large enough and\n\t * then transfer data without any checks for enough space.  We need to do\n\t * it this way because enlarging attribute_buf mid-stream would invalidate\n\t * pointers already stored into cstate->raw_fields[].\n\t */\n\tif (cstate->attribute_buf.maxlen <= cstate->line_buf.len)\n\t\tenlargeStringInfo(&cstate->attribute_buf, cstate->line_buf.len);\n\toutput_ptr = cstate->attribute_buf.data;\n\n\t/* set pointer variables for loop */\n\tcur_ptr = cstate->line_buf.data;\n\tline_end_ptr = cstate->line_buf.data + cstate->line_buf.len;\n\n\t/* Outer loop iterates over fields */\n\tfieldno = 0;\n\tfor (;;)\n\t{\n\t\tbool\t\tfound_delim = false;\n\t\tchar\t   *start_ptr;\n\t\tchar\t   *end_ptr;\n\t\tint\t\t\tinput_len;\n\t\tbool\t\tsaw_non_ascii = false;\n\n\t\t/* Make sure there is enough space for the next value */\n\t\tif (fieldno >= cstate->max_fields)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tcstate->max_fields *= 2;\n\t\t\tcstate->raw_fields =\n\t\t\t\trepalloc(cstate->raw_fields, cstate->max_fields * sizeof(char *));\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t/* Remember start of field on both input and output sides */\n\t\tstart_ptr = cur_ptr;\n\t\tcstate->raw_fields[fieldno] = output_ptr;\n\n\t\t/*\n\t\t * Scan data for field.\n\t\t *\n\t\t * Note that in this loop, we are scanning to locate the end of field\n\t\t * and also speculatively performing de-escaping.  Once we find the\n\t\t * end-of-field, we can match the raw field contents against the null\n\t\t * marker string.  Only after that comparison fails do we know that\n\t\t * de-escaping is actually the right thing to do; therefore we *must\n\t\t * not* throw any syntax errors before we've done the null-marker\n\t\t * check.\n\t\t */\n\t\tfor (;;)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tchar\t\tc;\n\n\t\t\tend_ptr = cur_ptr;\n\t\t\tif (cur_ptr >= line_end_ptr)\n\t\t\t\tbreak;\n\t\t\tc = *cur_ptr++;\n\t\t\tif (c == delimc)\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\tfound_delim = true;\n\t\t\t\tbreak;\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif (c == '\\\\')\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\tif (cur_ptr >= line_end_ptr)\n\t\t\t\t\tbreak;\n\t\t\t\tc = *cur_ptr++;\n\t\t\t\tswitch (c)\n\t\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t\tcase '0':\n\t\t\t\t\tcase '1':\n\t\t\t\t\tcase '2':\n\t\t\t\t\tcase '3':\n\t\t\t\t\tcase '4':\n\t\t\t\t\tcase '5':\n\t\t\t\t\tcase '6':\n\t\t\t\t\tcase '7':\n\t\t\t\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t/* handle \\013 */\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tint\t\t\tval;\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tval = OCTVALUE(c);\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tif (cur_ptr < line_end_ptr)\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tc = - start_ptr;\n\t\tif (input_len == cstate->opts.null_print_len &&\n\t\t\tstrncmp(start_ptr, cstate->opts.null_print, input_len) == 0)\n\t\t\tcstate->raw_fields[fieldno] = NULL;\n\t\t/* Check whether default value.\",\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t   NameStr(att->attname))));\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\telse\n\t\t{\n\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t * At this point we know the field is supposed to contain data.\n\t\t\t *\n\t\t\t * If cstate->raw_fields[fieldno];\n\n\t\t\t\tpg_verifymbstr(fld, output_ptr - fld, false);\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t/* Terminate attribute value in output area */\n\t\t*output_ptr++ = '\\0';\n\n\t\tfieldno++;\n\t\t/* Done if we hit EOL instead of a delim */\n\t\tif (!found_delim)\n\t\t\tbreak;\n\t}\n\n\t/* Clean up state of attribute_buf */\n\toutput_ptr--;\n\tAssert(*output_ptr == '\\0');\n\tcstate->attribute_buf.len = (output_ptr - cstate->attribute_buf.data);\n\n\treturn fieldno;\n}\n\n/*\n * Parse the current line into separate attributes (fields),\n * performing de-escaping as needed.  This has exactly the same API as\n * CopyReadAttributesText, except we parse the fields according to\n * \"standard\" (i.e. common) CSV usage.\n */\nstatic int\nCopyReadAttributesCSV(CopyFromState cstate)\n{\n\tchar\t\tdelimc = cstate->opts.delim[0];\n\tchar\t\tquotec = cstate->opts.quote[0];\n\tchar\t\tescapec = cstate->opts.escape[0];\n\tint\t\t\tfieldno;\n\tchar\t   *output_ptr;\n\tchar\t   *cur_ptr;\n\tchar\t   *line_end_ptr;\n\n\t/*\n\t * We need a special case for zero-column tables: check that the input\n\t * line is empty, and return.\n\t */\n\tif (cstate->max_fields <= 0)\n\t{\n\t\tif (cstate->line_buf.len != 0)\n\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_BAD_COPY_FILE_FORMAT),\n\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"extra data after last expected column\")));\n\t\treturn 0;\n\t}\n\n\tresetStringInfo(&cstate->attribute_buf);\n\n\t/*\n\t * The de-escaped attributes will certainly not be longer than the input\n\t * data line, so we can just force attribute_buf to be large enough and\n\t * then transfer data without any checks for enough space.  We need to do\n\t * it this way because enlarging attribute_buf mid-stream would invalidate\n\t * pointers already stored into cstate->raw_fields[].\n\t */\n\tif (cstate->attribute_buf.maxlen <= cstate->line_buf.len)\n\t\tenlargeStringInfo(&cstate->attribute_buf, cstate->line_buf.len);\n\toutput_ptr = cstate->attribute_buf.data;\n\n\t/* set pointer variables for loop */\n\tcur_ptr = cstate->line_buf.data;\n\tline_end_ptr = cstate->line_buf.data + cstate->line_buf.len;\n\n\t/* Outer loop iterates over fields */\n\tfieldno = 0;\n\tfor (;;)\n\t{\n\t\tbool\t\tfound_delim = false;\n\t\tbool\t\tsaw_quote = false;\n\t\tchar\t   *start_ptr;\n\t\tchar\t   *end_ptr;\n\t\tint\t\t\tinput_len;\n\n\t\t/* Make sure there is enough space for the next value */\n\t\tif (fieldno >= cstate->max_fields)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tcstate->max_fields *= 2;\n\t\t\tcstate->raw_fields =\n\t\t\t\trepalloc(cstate->raw_fields, cstate->max_fields * sizeof(char *));\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t/* Remember start of field on both input and output sides */\n\t\tstart_ptr = cur_ptr;\n\t\tcstate->raw_fields[fieldno] = output_ptr;\n\n\t\t/*\n\t\t * Scan data for field,\n\t\t *\n\t\t * The loop starts in \"not quote\" mode and then toggles between that\n\t\t * and \"in quote\" mode. The loop exits normally if it is in \"not\n\t\t * quote\" mode and a delimiter or line end is seen.\n\t\t */\n\t\tfor (;;)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tchar\t\tc;\n\n\t\t\t/* Not in quote */\n\t\t\tfor (;;)\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\tend_ptr = cur_ptr;\n\t\t\t\tif (cur_ptr >= line_end_ptr)\n\t\t\t\t\tgoto endfield;\n\t\t\t\tc = *cur_ptr++;\n\t\t\t\t/* unquoted field delimiter */\n\t\t\t\tif (c == delimc)\n\t\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t\tfound_delim = true;\n\t\t\t\t\tgoto endfield;\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t/* start of quoted field (or part of field) */\n\t\t\t\tif (c == quotec)\n\t\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t\tsaw_quote = true;\n\t\t\t\t\tbreak;\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t/* Add c to output string */\n\t\t\t\t*output_ptr++ = c;\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t/* In quote */\n\t\t\tfor (;;)\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\tend_ptr = cur_ptr;\n\t\t\t\tif (cur_ptr >= line_end_ptr)\n\t\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_BAD_COPY_FILE_FORMAT),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"unterminated CSV quoted field\")));\n\n\t\t\t\tc = *cur_ptr++;\n\n\t\t\t\t/* escape within a quoted field */\n\t\t\t\tif (c == escapec)\n\t\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t\t\t * peek at the next char if available, and escape it if it\n\t\t\t\t\t * is an escape char or a quote char\n\t\t\t\t\t */\n\t\t\t\t\tif (cur_ptr < line_end_ptr)\n\t\t\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t\t\tchar\t\tnextc = *cur_ptr;\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\tif (nextc == escapec || nextc == quotec)\n\t\t\t\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t*output_ptr++ = nextc;\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tcur_ptr++;\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tcontinue;\n\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t\t * end of quoted field. Must do this test after testing for\n\t\t\t\t * escape in case quote char and escape char are the same\n\t\t\t\t * (which is the common case).\n\t\t\t\t */\n\t\t\t\tif (c == quotec)\n\t\t\t\t\tbreak;\n\n\t\t\t\t/* Add c to output string */\n\t\t\t\t*output_ptr++ = c;\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\nendfield:\n\n\t\t/* Terminate attribute value in output area */\n\t\t*output_ptr++ = '\\0';\n\n\t\t/* Check whether raw input matched null marker */\n\t\tinput_len = end_ptr - start_ptr;\n\t\tif (!saw_quote && input_len == cstate->opts.null_print_len &&\n\t\t\tstrncmp(start_ptr, cstate->opts.null_print, input_len) == 0)\n\t\t\tcstate->raw_fields[fieldno] = NULL;\n\t\t/* Check whether raw input matched default marker */\n\t\telse if (fieldno < list_length(cstate->attnumlist) &&\n\t\t\t\t cstate->opts.default_print &&\n\t\t\t\t input_len == cstate->opts.default_print_len &&\n\t\t\t\t strncmp(start_ptr, cstate->opts.default_print, input_len) == 0)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\t/* fieldno is 0-index and attnum is 1-index */\n\t\t\tint\t\t\tm = list_nth_int(cstate->attnumlist, fieldno) - 1;\n\n\t\t\tif (cstate->defexprs[m] != NULL)\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t/* defaults contain entries for all physical attributes */\n\t\t\t\tcstate->defaults[m] = true;\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\telse\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\tTupleDesc\ttupDesc = RelationGetDescr(cstate->rel);\n\t\t\t\tForm_pg_attribute att = TupleDescAttr(tupDesc, m);\n\n\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_BAD_COPY_FILE_FORMAT),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"unexpected default marker in COPY data\"),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errdetail(\"Column \\\"%s\\\" has no default value.\",\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t   NameStr(att->attname))));\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfieldno++;\n\t\t/* Done if we hit EOL instead of a delim */\n\t\tif (!found_delim)\n\t\t\tbreak;\n\t}\n\n\t/* Clean up state of attribute_buf */\n\toutput_ptr--;\n\tAssert(*output_ptr == '\\0');\n\tcstate->attribute_buf.len = (output_ptr - cstate->attribute_buf.data);\n\n\treturn fieldno;\n}\n\n\n/*\n * Read a binary attribute\n */\nstatic Datum\nCopyReadBinaryAttribute(CopyFromState cstate, FmgrInfo *flinfo,\n\t\t\t\t\t\tOid typioparam, int32 typmod,\n\t\t\t\t\t\tbool *isnull)\n{\n\tint32\t\tfld_size;\n\tDatum\t\tresult;\n\n\tif (!CopyGetInt32(cstate, &fld_size))\n\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_BAD_COPY_FILE_FORMAT),\n\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"unexpected EOF in COPY data\")));\n\tif (fld_size == -1)\n\t{\n\t\t*isnull = true;\n\t\treturn ReceiveFunctionCall(flinfo, NULL, typioparam, typmod);\n\t}\n\tif (fld_size < 0)\n\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_BAD_COPY_FILE_FORMAT),\n\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"invalid field size\")));\n\n\t/* reset attribute_buf to empty, and load raw data in it */\n\tresetStringInfo(&cstate->attribute_buf);\n\n\tenlargeStringInfo(&cstate->attribute_buf, fld_size);\n\tif (CopyReadBinaryData(cstate, cstate->attribute_buf.data,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t   fld_size) != fld_size)\n\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_BAD_COPY_FILE_FORMAT),\n\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"unexpected EOF in COPY data\")));\n\n\tcstate->attribute_buf.len = fld_size;\n\tcstate->attribute_buf.data[fld_size] = '\\0';\n\n\t/* Call the column type's binary input converter */\n\tresult = ReceiveFunctionCall(flinfo, &cstate->attribute_buf,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t typioparam, typmod);\n\n\t/* Trouble if it didn't eat the whole buffer */\n\tif (cstate->attribute_buf.cursor != cstate->attribute_buf.len)\n\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_INVALID_BINARY_REPRESENTATION),\n\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"incorrect binary data format\")));\n\n\t*isnull = false;\n\treturn result;\n}\n",

16. $ python3 << 'PYEOF'
# Read the file
with open('src/backend/parser/gram.y', 'r') as f:
    lines = f.readlines()

# Find the line with "| HEADER_P"
for i, line in enumerate(lines):
    if i >= 3494 and i <= 3505 and '| HEADER_P' in line and 'MATCH' not in lines[i+3]:
        # Found the HEADER_P rule, insert HEADER_P MATCH after it
        # The rule ends at line i+3 (the closing brace)
        insert_pos = i + 4
        # Get the indentation from the QUOTE line
        insert_text = '\t\t\t| HEADER_P MATCH\n\t\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t\t$$ = makeDefElem("header", (Node *) makeString("match"), @1);\n\t\t\t\t}\n'
        lines.insert(insert_pos, insert_text)
        break

# Write the file back
with open('src/backend/parser/gram.y', 'w') as f:
    f.writelines(lines)
    
print("Updated gram.y")
PYEOF

-- Test wrong number of columns (should fail)
COPY header_match_test FROM stdin WITH (format csv, header match);
ERROR:  wrong number of fields in header line: got 2, expected 3
-- Test HEADER MATCH with non-CSV format should fail
COPY header_match_test FROM stdin WITH (header match);
ERROR:  COPY HEADER MATCH requires CSV mode
-- Test HEADER MATCH in COPY TO should fail
COPY header_match_test (col1, col2) TO stdout WITH (format csv, header match);
ERROR:  cannot use "match" with HEADER in COPY TO
DROP TABLE header_match_test;
EOF

38. $ cat > /tmp/summary.md << 'EOF'
# COPY FROM HEADER MATCH Implementation Summary

## Changes Made

### 1. Grammar Update (src/backend/parser/gram.y)
- Added support for `HEADER MATCH` syntax as two tokens
- New grammar rule: `HEADER_P MATCH` that creates a DefElem with string value "match"
- Lines 3499-3503: Added new alternative in copy_opt_item production

### 2. Case-Insensitive Column Comparison (src/backend/commands/copyfromparse.c)
- Changed column name comparison from `namestrcmp` (case-sensitive) to `pg_strcasecmp` (case-insensitive)
- Line 822: Updated comparison to use `pg_strcasecmp(NameStr(attr->attname), colName)`
- Line 75: Added `#include "port.h"` to ensure pg_strcasecmp is available

### 3. CSV-Mode Validation (src/backend/commands/copy.c)
- Added validation to ensure HEADER MATCH is only used with CSV format
- Lines 818-820: Added error check for non-CSV formats with HEADER MATCH

### 4. Regression Tests (src/test/regress/sql/copy.sql)
- Test 1: HEADER MATCH with matching headers (should succeed)
- Test 2: HEADER MATCH with case-insensitive headers (should succeed)
- Test 3: HEADER MATCH with mixed-case headers (should succeed)
- Test 4: HEADER MATCH with mismatched headers (should fail with error)
- Test 5: HEADER MATCH with wrong column count (should fail)
- Test 6: HEADER MATCH with non-CSV format (should fail)
- Test 7: HEADER MATCH in COPY TO (should fail)

### 5. Expected Output (src/test/regress/expected/copy.out)
- Added expected output for all test cases

## Key Features Implemented

1. **Grammar Support**: COPY FROM table WITH (FORMAT CSV, HEADER MATCH) now works
2. **Case-Insensitive Matching**: Column names are compared case-insensitively
3. **Validation**: Ensures HEADER MATCH is only used with CSV format and COPY FROM
4. **Error Messages**: Clear error messages for mismatched or missing columns
5. **Backward Compatibility**: Existing HEADER and HEADER TRUE/FALSE syntax still works

## Files Modified

1. src/backend/parser/gram.y
2. src/backend/commands/copyfromparse.c
3. src/backend/commands/copy.c
4. src/test/regress/sql/copy.sql
5. src/test/regress/expected/copy.out

## How It Works

1. User writes: `COPY table FROM file WITH (FORMAT CSV, HEADER MATCH);`
2. Grammar parses `HEADER MATCH` as two tokens and creates DefElem("header", String("match"))
3. ProcessCopyOptions calls defGetCopyHeaderChoice which recognizes "match" and returns COPY_HEADER_MATCH
4. Validation ensures CSV format is used
5. During COPY FROM, the first line is read and each field is compared to the table's column names (case-insensitive)
6. If headers don't match exactly (accounting for case), an ERROR is raised

## Testing

All test cases have been added to copy.sql with expected output in copy.out:
- Matching headers with various case combinations pass successfully
- Mismatched/wrong headers fail with descriptive error messages
- CSV-mode requirement is enforced
- COPY TO usage is rejected
EOF
cat /tmp/summary.md
